**GT numerical expression:**
`0.1404201690960543*(-1 + P/4.5321236760653205)*(1 - P/78.49071311458529)*P + 0.1404201690960543*P/t**4.5321236760653205`

(-1 + P/4.532124)(1 - P/78.49071) = -1 + P/78.49071 + P/4.532124 - P²/(4.532124 × 78.49071)

= -0.140420*P + 0.140420*P²/78.49071 + 0.140420*P²/4.532124 - 0.140420*P³/355.617

where c₀, c₁, c₂ are specific constants and c₃ = 0.140420.

The GT structure is: **P³·(const) + P²·(const) + P·(const) + P·(const)/t^(const)**

Let me check candidates carefully:

**Candidate 49:** `P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P**2*c2 + P*c3 + P*c4 + c5*t**c6*exp(P*c7)`

**Candidate 28:** `P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P**c2*c3*t**c4 + c5 + c6*exp(c7*t)`

GT: c0*(-c1 + P/c2)*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*P/t**c6

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) and compare each candidate to it.

## Ground Truth Analysis

The GT is:
$$f(t, P) = 0.1404 \cdot (-1 + P/4.532) \cdot (1 - P/78.49) \cdot P + 0.1404 \cdot P / t^{4.532}$$

Let me expand the polynomial part:
$$(-1 + P/4.532)(1 - P/78.49) = -1 + P/78.49 + P/4.532 - P^2/(4.532 \cdot 78.49)$$

So the first term becomes:
$$0.1404 \cdot P \cdot [-1 + P/78.49 + P/4.532 - P^2/(4.532 \cdot 78.49)]$$
$$= 0.1404 \cdot [-P + P^2/78.49 + P^2/4.532 - P^3/(4.532 \cdot 78.49)]$$

This gives us:
$$f(t, P) = -0.1404 \cdot P^3/(4.532 \cdot 78.49) + 0.1404 \cdot P^2 \cdot (1/78.49 + 1/4.532) - 0.1404 \cdot P + 0.1404 \cdot P/t^{4.532}$$

So the GT has the form:
$$f(t, P) = a \cdot P^3 + b \cdot P^2 + c \cdot P + d \cdot P/t^{4.532}$$

where $a, b, c, d$ are specific constants. The key structural elements are:
- **P³ term** (cubic in P)
- **P² term** (quadratic in P)
- **P term** (linear in P)
- **P/t^{4.532} term** (P times a power of t)

No constant term (independent of P), no exponential terms, no log terms, no trigonometric terms.

Now let me check each candidate:

### Candidate 1: P³c0 + P²c1 + P²c2 + Pc3 + c4·t^c5·exp(P·c6)

Structure: P³ + P² + P + t^c5·exp(P·c6)

The GT has P/t^{4.532} as the last term. Can c4·t^c5·exp(P·c6) equal d·P/t^{4.532}?

exp(P·c6) cannot equal P for all P (exponential vs polynomial). Setting c6=0 gives exp(0)=1, then c4·t^c5 which is just a function of t, not P·f(t). We need the term to be proportional to P, but exp(P·c6) with c6=0 is constant in P, and with c6≠0 is exponential in P. **No match.**
